[90m16:49:34:139[0m [34m[client-request-interceptor:on][0m adding "request" event listener: async ({ request, requestId, controller }) => {
        const response = await handleRequest(
          request,
          requestId,
          this.handlersController.currentHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("RequestHandler")),
          this.resolvedOptions,
          this.emitter,
          {
            onPassthroughResponse(request2) {
              const acceptHeader = request2.headers.get("accept");
              if (acceptHeader) {
                const nextAcceptHeader = acceptHeader.replace(
                  /(,\s+)?msw\/passthrough/,
                  ""
                );
                if (nextAcceptHeader) {
                  request2.headers.set("accept", nextAcceptHeader);
                } else {
                  request2.headers.delete("accept");
                }
              }
            }
          }
        );
        if (response) {
          controller.respondWith(response);
        }
        return;
      }

[90m16:49:34:140[0m [34m[websocket:on][0m adding "connection" event listener: async (connection) => {
    const handlers = options.getHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("EventHandler"));
    if (handlers.length > 0) {
      options?.onMockedConnection(connection);
      await Promise.all(
        handlers.map((handler) => {
          return handler.run(connection);
        })
      );
      return;
    }
    const request = new Request(connection.client.url, {
      headers: {
        upgrade: "websocket",
        connection: "upgrade"
      }
    });
    await onUnhandledRequest(
      request,
      options.getUnhandledRequestStrategy()
    ).catch((error) => {
      const errorEvent = new Event("error");
      Object.defineProperty(errorEvent, "cause", {
        enumerable: true,
        configurable: false,
        value: error
      });
      connection.client.socket.dispatchEvent(errorEvent);
    });
    options?.onPassthroughConnection(connection);
    connection.server.connect();
  }

[90m16:49:34:989[0m [34m[client-request-interceptor:on][0m adding "request" event listener: async ({ request, requestId, controller }) => {
        const response = await handleRequest(
          request,
          requestId,
          this.handlersController.currentHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("RequestHandler")),
          this.resolvedOptions,
          this.emitter,
          {
            onPassthroughResponse(request2) {
              const acceptHeader = request2.headers.get("accept");
              if (acceptHeader) {
                const nextAcceptHeader = acceptHeader.replace(
                  /(,\s+)?msw\/passthrough/,
                  ""
                );
                if (nextAcceptHeader) {
                  request2.headers.set("accept", nextAcceptHeader);
                } else {
                  request2.headers.delete("accept");
                }
              }
            }
          }
        );
        if (response) {
          controller.respondWith(response);
        }
        return;
      }

[90m16:49:34:991[0m [34m[websocket:on][0m adding "connection" event listener: async (connection) => {
    const handlers = options.getHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("EventHandler"));
    if (handlers.length > 0) {
      options?.onMockedConnection(connection);
      await Promise.all(
        handlers.map((handler) => {
          return handler.run(connection);
        })
      );
      return;
    }
    const request = new Request(connection.client.url, {
      headers: {
        upgrade: "websocket",
        connection: "upgrade"
      }
    });
    await onUnhandledRequest(
      request,
      options.getUnhandledRequestStrategy()
    ).catch((error) => {
      const errorEvent = new Event("error");
      Object.defineProperty(errorEvent, "cause", {
        enumerable: true,
        configurable: false,
        value: error
      });
      connection.client.socket.dispatchEvent(errorEvent);
    });
    options?.onPassthroughConnection(connection);
    connection.server.connect();
  }

[90m16:49:34:994[0m [34m[websocket:on][0m adding "connection" event listener: async (connection) => {
    const handlers = options.getHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("EventHandler"));
    if (handlers.length > 0) {
      options?.onMockedConnection(connection);
      await Promise.all(
        handlers.map((handler) => {
          return handler.run(connection);
        })
      );
      return;
    }
    const request = new Request(connection.client.url, {
      headers: {
        upgrade: "websocket",
        connection: "upgrade"
      }
    });
    await onUnhandledRequest(
      request,
      options.getUnhandledRequestStrategy()
    ).catch((error) => {
      const errorEvent = new Event("error");
      Object.defineProperty(errorEvent, "cause", {
        enumerable: true,
        configurable: false,
        value: error
      });
      connection.client.socket.dispatchEvent(errorEvent);
    });
    options?.onPassthroughConnection(connection);
    connection.server.connect();
  }

          request,
          requestId,
          this.handlersController.currentHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("RequestHandler")),
          this.resolvedOptions,
          this.emitter,
          {

                }
              }
            }
          }
        );

          controller.respondWith(response);
        }
        return;
      }

[90m16:49:35:92[0m [34m[websocket:on][0m adding "connection" event listener: async (connection) => {
    const handlers = options.getHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("EventHandler"));
    if (handlers.length > 0) {
      options?.onMockedConnection(connection);
      await Promise.all(
        handlers.map((handler) => {
          return handler.run(connection);
        })
      );
      return;
    }
    const request = new Request(connection.client.url, {
      headers: {
        upgrade: "websocket",
        connection: "upgrade"
      }
    });
    await onUnhandledRequest(
      request,
      options.getUnhandledRequestStrategy()
    ).catch((error) => {
      const errorEvent = new Event("error");
      Object.defineProperty(errorEvent, "cause", {
        enumerable: true,
        configurable: false,
        value: error
      });
      connection.client.socket.dispatchEvent(errorEvent);
    });
    options?.onPassthroughConnection(connection);
    connection.server.connect();
  }

[90m16:49:40:488[0m [34m[websocket:on][0m adding "connection" event listener: async (connection) => {
    const handlers = options.getHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("EventHandler"));
    if (handlers.length > 0) {
      options?.onMockedConnection(connection);
      await Promise.all(
        handlers.map((handler) => {
          return handler.run(connection);
        })
      );
      return;
    }
    const request = new Request(connection.client.url, {
      headers: {
        upgrade: "websocket",
        connection: "upgrade"
      }
    });
    await onUnhandledRequest(
      request,
      options.getUnhandledRequestStrategy()
    ).catch((error) => {
      const errorEvent = new Event("error");
      Object.defineProperty(errorEvent, "cause", {
        enumerable: true,
        configurable: false,
        value: error
      });
      connection.client.socket.dispatchEvent(errorEvent);
    });
    options?.onPassthroughConnection(connection);
    connection.server.connect();
  }

                }
              }
            }
          }
        );

          controller.respondWith(response);
        }
        return;
      }

[90m16:49:42:747[0m [34m[websocket:on][0m adding "connection" event listener: async (connection) => {
    const handlers = options.getHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("EventHandler"));
    if (handlers.length > 0) {
      options?.onMockedConnection(connection);
      await Promise.all(
        handlers.map((handler) => {
          return handler.run(connection);
        })
      );
      return;
    }
    const request = new Request(connection.client.url, {
      headers: {
        upgrade: "websocket",
        connection: "upgrade"
      }
    });
    await onUnhandledRequest(
      request,
      options.getUnhandledRequestStrategy()
    ).catch((error) => {
      const errorEvent = new Event("error");
      Object.defineProperty(errorEvent, "cause", {
        enumerable: true,
        configurable: false,
        value: error
      });
      connection.client.socket.dispatchEvent(errorEvent);
    });
    options?.onPassthroughConnection(connection);
    connection.server.connect();
  }

[90m16:49:42:916[0m [34m[client-request-interceptor:on][0m adding "request" event listener: async ({ request, requestId, controller }) => {
        const response = await handleRequest(
          request,
          requestId,
          this.handlersController.currentHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("RequestHandler")),
          this.resolvedOptions,
          this.emitter,
          {
            onPassthroughResponse(request2) {
              const acceptHeader = request2.headers.get("accept");
              if (acceptHeader) {
                const nextAcceptHeader = acceptHeader.replace(
                  /(,\s+)?msw\/passthrough/,
                  ""
                );
                if (nextAcceptHeader) {
                  request2.headers.set("accept", nextAcceptHeader);
                } else {
                  request2.headers.delete("accept");
                }
              }
            }
          }
        );
        if (response) {
          controller.respondWith(response);
        }
        return;
      }

[90m16:49:42:917[0m [34m[websocket:on][0m adding "connection" event listener: async (connection) => {
    const handlers = options.getHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("EventHandler"));
    if (handlers.length > 0) {
      options?.onMockedConnection(connection);
      await Promise.all(
        handlers.map((handler) => {
          return handler.run(connection);
        })
      );
      return;
    }
    const request = new Request(connection.client.url, {
      headers: {
        upgrade: "websocket",
        connection: "upgrade"
      }
    });
    await onUnhandledRequest(
      request,
      options.getUnhandledRequestStrategy()
    ).catch((error) => {
      const errorEvent = new Event("error");
      Object.defineProperty(errorEvent, "cause", {
        enumerable: true,
        configurable: false,
        value: error
      });
      connection.client.socket.dispatchEvent(errorEvent);
    });
    options?.onPassthroughConnection(connection);
    connection.server.connect();
  }

[90m16:49:43:597[0m [34m[websocket:on][0m adding "connection" event listener: async (connection) => {
    const handlers = options.getHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("EventHandler"));
    if (handlers.length > 0) {
      options?.onMockedConnection(connection);
      await Promise.all(
        handlers.map((handler) => {
          return handler.run(connection);
        })
      );
      return;
    }
    const request = new Request(connection.client.url, {
      headers: {
        upgrade: "websocket",
        connection: "upgrade"
      }
    });
    await onUnhandledRequest(
      request,
      options.getUnhandledRequestStrategy()
    ).catch((error) => {
      const errorEvent = new Event("error");
      Object.defineProperty(errorEvent, "cause", {
        enumerable: true,
        configurable: false,
        value: error
      });
      connection.client.socket.dispatchEvent(errorEvent);
    });
    options?.onPassthroughConnection(connection);
    connection.server.connect();
  }

      });

    });

    connection.server.connect();

      }
    });

        enumerable: true,
        configurable: false,

      });
      connection.client.socket.dispatchEvent(errorEvent);
    });
    options?.onPassthroughConnection(connection);
    connection.server.connect();

[90m16:49:49:634[0m [34m[websocket:on][0m adding "connection" event listener: async (connection) => {
    const handlers = options.getHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("EventHandler"));
    if (handlers.length > 0) {
      options?.onMockedConnection(connection);
      await Promise.all(
        handlers.map((handler) => {
          return handler.run(connection);
        })
      );
      return;
    }
    const request = new Request(connection.client.url, {
      headers: {
        upgrade: "websocket",
        connection: "upgrade"
      }
    });
    await onUnhandledRequest(
      request,
      options.getUnhandledRequestStrategy()
    ).catch((error) => {
      const errorEvent = new Event("error");
      Object.defineProperty(errorEvent, "cause", {
        enumerable: true,
        configurable: false,
        value: error
      });
      connection.client.socket.dispatchEvent(errorEvent);
    });
    options?.onPassthroughConnection(connection);
    connection.server.connect();
  }

        configurable: false,

      });

    });
    options?.onPassthroughConnection(connection);
    connection.server.connect();

      }

      options.getUnhandledRequestStrategy()

      Object.defineProperty(errorEvent, "cause", {
        enumerable: true,
        configurable: false,
        value: error
      });
      connection.client.socket.dispatchEvent(errorEvent);
    });
    options?.onPassthroughConnection(connection);
    connection.server.connect();

[90m16:49:50:333[0m [34m[websocket:on][0m adding "connection" event listener: async (connection) => {
    const handlers = options.getHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("EventHandler"));
    if (handlers.length > 0) {
      options?.onMockedConnection(connection);
      await Promise.all(
        handlers.map((handler) => {
          return handler.run(connection);
        })
      );
      return;
    }
    const request = new Request(connection.client.url, {
      headers: {
        upgrade: "websocket",
        connection: "upgrade"
      }
    });
    await onUnhandledRequest(
      request,
      options.getUnhandledRequestStrategy()
    ).catch((error) => {
      const errorEvent = new Event("error");
      Object.defineProperty(errorEvent, "cause", {
        enumerable: true,
        configurable: false,
        value: error
      });
      connection.client.socket.dispatchEvent(errorEvent);
    });
    options?.onPassthroughConnection(connection);
    connection.server.connect();
  }

[90m16:49:50:806[0m [34m[websocket:on][0m adding "connection" event listener: async (connection) => {
    const handlers = options.getHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("EventHandler"));
    if (handlers.length > 0) {
      options?.onMockedConnection(connection);
      await Promise.all(
        handlers.map((handler) => {
          return handler.run(connection);
        })
      );
      return;
    }
    const request = new Request(connection.client.url, {
      headers: {
        upgrade: "websocket",
        connection: "upgrade"
      }
    });
    await onUnhandledRequest(
      request,
      options.getUnhandledRequestStrategy()
    ).catch((error) => {
      const errorEvent = new Event("error");
      Object.defineProperty(errorEvent, "cause", {
        enumerable: true,
        configurable: false,
        value: error
      });
      connection.client.socket.dispatchEvent(errorEvent);
    });
    options?.onPassthroughConnection(connection);
    connection.server.connect();
  }

[90m16:49:51:631[0m [34m[websocket:on][0m adding "connection" event listener: async (connection) => {
    const handlers = options.getHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("EventHandler"));
    if (handlers.length > 0) {
      options?.onMockedConnection(connection);
      await Promise.all(
        handlers.map((handler) => {
          return handler.run(connection);
        })
      );
      return;
    }
    const request = new Request(connection.client.url, {
      headers: {
        upgrade: "websocket",
        connection: "upgrade"
      }
    });
    await onUnhandledRequest(
      request,
      options.getUnhandledRequestStrategy()
    ).catch((error) => {
      const errorEvent = new Event("error");
      Object.defineProperty(errorEvent, "cause", {
        enumerable: true,
        configurable: false,
        value: error
      });
      connection.client.socket.dispatchEvent(errorEvent);
    });
    options?.onPassthroughConnection(connection);
    connection.server.connect();
  }

[90m16:49:53:538[0m [34m[websocket:on][0m adding "connection" event listener: async (connection) => {
    const handlers = options.getHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("EventHandler"));
    if (handlers.length > 0) {
      options?.onMockedConnection(connection);
      await Promise.all(
        handlers.map((handler) => {
          return handler.run(connection);
        })
      );
      return;
    }
    const request = new Request(connection.client.url, {
      headers: {
        upgrade: "websocket",
        connection: "upgrade"
      }
    });
    await onUnhandledRequest(
      request,
      options.getUnhandledRequestStrategy()
    ).catch((error) => {
      const errorEvent = new Event("error");
      Object.defineProperty(errorEvent, "cause", {
        enumerable: true,
        configurable: false,
        value: error
      });
      connection.client.socket.dispatchEvent(errorEvent);
    });
    options?.onPassthroughConnection(connection);
    connection.server.connect();
  }
